<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ol><li>2 first published by Wildt of Cracow. (The Wildt first edition has been digitized: <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/oclc/54448303">WorldCat</a></span>.) Its date is confirmed @ <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://anno.onb.ac.at/cgi-content/anno-buch?apm=0&amp;aid=1000001&amp;bd=0001852&amp;teil=0203&amp;seite=00000134&amp;zoom=1">Hofmeister's <i>Monatsbericht</i> (1852), p.134</a></span> and in the side-comments @ <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://en.chopin.nifc.pl/chopin/first_editions/detail/id/51">http://en.chopin.nifc.pl/chopin/first_editions/detail/id/51</a>. Op.69 No.1 apparently first published by Schlesinger and Meissonnier in 1855, though.
</li></ol>
